[1/35] CQ04: Which of the named and published algorithms does this tool use?
======================================================================
<?xml version="1.0"?>
<rdf:RDF xml:base="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#"
         xmlns:owl="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
         xmlns:rdf="http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#"
         xmlns:rdfs="http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#"
         xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#">

  <owl:Ontology rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#"/>

  <!-- owl:Class declarations -->

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Tool">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A software application or computational system.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Tool</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Algorithm">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A defined set of rules or procedures for solving a problem or accomplishing a task.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Algorithm</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

  <!-- owl:ObjectProperty declarations -->

<owl:ObjectProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#usesAlgorithm">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Relates a tool to an algorithm that it implements or utilizes.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">uses algorithm</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Tool"/>
  <rdfs:range rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Algorithm"/>
</owl:ObjectProperty>

</rdf:RDF>

  <!-- owl:ObjectProperty declarations -->

</owl:ObjectProperty>

<owl:ObjectProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#modifiesAlgorithm">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Relates an algorithm modification to the algorithm being modified.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">modifies algorithm</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#AlgorithmModification"/>
  <rdfs:range rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Algorithm"/>
</owl:ObjectProperty>

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">performed by tool</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#AlgorithmModification"/>
  <rdfs:range rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Tool"/>
</owl:ObjectProperty>

  <!-- owl:DatatypeProperty declarations -->

<owl:DatatypeProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#modificationDate">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">The date and time when the algorithm modification occurred.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">modification date</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#AlgorithmModification"/>
  <rdfs:range rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#xsd:dateTime"/>
</owl:DatatypeProperty>

<owl:DatatypeProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#modificationDescription">

         xmlns:owl="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
         xmlns:rdf="http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#"
         xmlns:rdfs="http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#"
         xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#">

  <owl:Ontology rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#"/>

  <!-- owl:Class declarations -->

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Tool">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A software application or computational system.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Tool</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Algorithm">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A defined set of rules or procedures for solving a problem or accomplishing a task.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Algorithm</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#AlgorithmModification">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents a modification event to an algorithm used by a tool.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Algorithm Modification</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Feature">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A software feature or capability provided by a tool.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Feature</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#XMLEditing">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A software feature that enables the creation, modification, or formatting of XML documents.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">XML Editing</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:subClassOf rdf:resource='http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Feature'/>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#SoftwareType">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">The category or type of software application (e.g., API, Desktop application).</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Software Type</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Task">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A specific job, operation, or function that a tool can execute.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Task</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#UserNeed">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A requirement or objective that a user wants to achieve.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">User Need</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Data">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A piece of information or content generated by a tool or user.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Data</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#DataUsage">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents the usage of data with a software tool to support a specific task.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Data Usage</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#DataFormat">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents a specific data format (e.g., XML, JSON, CSV) used for input or output.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Data Format</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#CelFormat">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents the .cel file format used in microarray data.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">CEL Format</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:subClassOf rdf:resource='http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#DataFormat'/>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Export">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents an export operation performed by a tool, linking an input format to an output format.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Export</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#OpenFormat">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents an open, publicly documented data format.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Open Format</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:subClassOf rdf:resource='http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#DataFormat'/>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#ProprietaryFormat">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents a proprietary or closed data format.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Proprietary Format</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:subClassOf rdf:resource='http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#DataFormat'/>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#CSVFormat">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents the Comma-Separated Values (CSV) open data format.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">CSV Format</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:subClassOf rdf:resource='http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#OpenFormat'/>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#TXTFormat">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents the plain text (TXT) open data format.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">TXT Format</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:subClassOf rdf:resource='http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#OpenFormat'/>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Help">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents assistance, documentation, or support resources provided for a software tool.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Help</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Developer">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">An individual or organization that creates or develops a software tool.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Developer</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#User">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A person or entity that interacts with or uses the software tools.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">User</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

  <!-- owl:ObjectProperty declarations -->

<owl:ObjectProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#usesAlgorithm">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Relates a tool to an algorithm that it implements or utilizes.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">uses algorithm</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Tool"/>
  <rdfs:range rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Algorithm"/>
</owl:ObjectProperty>

<owl:ObjectProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#modifiesAlgorithm">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Relates an algorithm modification to the algorithm being modified.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">modifies algorithm</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#AlgorithmModification"/>
  <rdfs:range rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Algorithm"/>
</owl:ObjectProperty>

<owl:ObjectProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#performedByTool">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Relates an algorithm modification to the tool that performed it.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">performed by tool</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#AlgorithmModification"/>
  <rdfs:range rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Tool"/>
</owl:ObjectProperty>

<owl:ObjectProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#providesFeature">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Relates a tool to a feature that it provides.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">provides feature</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Tool"/>
  <rdfs:range rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Feature"/>
</owl:ObjectProperty>

<owl:ObjectProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#hasSoftwareType">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Relates a tool to its software type.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">has software type</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Tool"/>
  <rdfs:range rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#SoftwareType"/>
</owl:ObjectProperty>

<owl:ObjectProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#performsTask">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Relates a tool to a task that it can perform.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">performs task</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Tool"/>
  <rdfs:range rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Task"/>
</owl:ObjectProperty>

<owl:ObjectProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#satisfiesNeed">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Relates a task to the user need it satisfies.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">satisfies need</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Task"/>
  <rdfs:range rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#UserNeed"/>
</owl:ObjectProperty>

<owl:ObjectProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#createdBy">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Relates a piece of data to the software tool that created it.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">created by</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Data"/>
  <rdfs:range rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Tool"/>
</owl:ObjectProperty>

<owl:ObjectProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#hasData">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Relates a data usage event to the data involved.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">has data</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#DataUsage"/>

</owl:ObjectProperty>

<owl:ObjectProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#hasTool">

</owl:ObjectProperty>

</owl:ObjectProperty>

<owl:ObjectProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#hasInputFormat">

  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Tool"/>

  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Export"/>

<owl:ObjectProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#exportedInModification">

  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#AlgorithmModification"/>
  <rdfs:range rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#xsd:string"/>
</owl:DatatypeProperty>

  <!-- owl:Class declarations -->

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Tool">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A software application or computational system.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Tool</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Algorithm">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A defined set of rules or procedures for solving a problem or accomplishing a task.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Algorithm</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#AlgorithmModification">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents a modification event to an algorithm used by a tool.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Algorithm Modification</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Feature">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A software feature or capability provided by a tool.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Feature</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#XMLEditing">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A software feature that enables the creation, modification, or formatting of XML documents.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">XML Editing</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:subClassOf rdf:resource='http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Feature'/>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#SoftwareType">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">The category or type of software application (e.g., API, Desktop application).</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Software Type</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Task">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A specific job, operation, or function that a tool can execute.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Task</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#UserNeed">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A requirement or objective that a user wants to achieve.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">User Need</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Data">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A piece of information or content generated by a tool or user.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Data</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#DataUsage">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents the usage of data with a software tool to support a specific task.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Data Usage</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#DataFormat">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents a specific data format (e.g., XML, JSON, CSV) used for input or output.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Data Format</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#CelFormat">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents the .cel file format used in microarray data.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">CEL Format</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:subClassOf rdf:resource='http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#DataFormat'/>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Export">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents an export operation performed by a tool, linking an input format to an output format.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Export</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#OpenFormat">

</owl:Class>

</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#CSVFormat">

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">CSV Format</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:subClassOf rdf:resource='http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#OpenFormat'/>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#TXTFormat">

</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Developer">

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#User">

</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Version">

</owl:Class>

</owl:Class>

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Tool</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Algorithm">

  <owl:Ontology rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#"/>

  <!-- owl:Class declarations -->

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Tool">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A software application or computational system.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Tool</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Algorithm">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A defined set of rules or procedures for solving a problem or accomplishing a task.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Algorithm</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#AlgorithmModification">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents a modification event to an algorithm used by a tool.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Algorithm Modification</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Feature">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A software feature or capability provided by a tool.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Feature</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#XMLEditing">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A software feature that enables the creation, modification, or formatting of XML documents.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">XML Editing</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:subClassOf rdf:resource='http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Feature'/>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#SoftwareType">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">The category or type of software application (e.g., API, Desktop application).</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Software Type</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Task">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A specific job, operation, or function that a tool can execute.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Task</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#UserNeed">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A requirement or objective that a user wants to achieve.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">User Need</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Data">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A piece of information or content generated by a tool or user.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Data</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#DataUsage">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents the usage of data with a software tool to support a specific task.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Data Usage</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#DataFormat">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents a specific data format (e.g., XML, JSON, CSV) used for input or output.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Data Format</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#CelFormat">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents the .cel file format used in microarray data.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">CEL Format</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:subClassOf rdf:resource='http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#DataFormat'/>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Export">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents an export operation performed by a tool, linking an input format to an output format.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Export</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#OpenFormat">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents an open, publicly documented data format.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Open Format</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:subClassOf rdf:resource='http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#DataFormat'/>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#ProprietaryFormat">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents a proprietary or closed data format.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Proprietary Format</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:subClassOf rdf:resource='http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#DataFormat'/>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#CSVFormat">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents the Comma-Separated Values (CSV) open data format.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">CSV Format</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:subClassOf rdf:resource='http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#OpenFormat'/>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#TXTFormat">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents the plain text (TXT) open data format.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">TXT Format</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:subClassOf rdf:resource='http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#OpenFormat'/>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Help">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents assistance, documentation, or support resources provided for a software tool.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Help</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Developer">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">An individual or organization that creates or develops a software tool.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Developer</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#User">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A person or entity that interacts with or uses the software tools.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">User</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Version">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents a specific release or version of a software tool.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Version</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#VersionRelease">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Represents the release event of a specific version of a software tool.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Version Release</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Community">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A group of individuals or organizations that collaboratively develop or maintain software.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Community</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#License">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A legal instrument granting rights to use, modify, and distribute software.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">License</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Permissiveness">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">The degree to which a license allows free use, modification, and distribution of software.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Permissiveness</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#ProgrammingLanguage">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A programming language in which a software tool is implemented.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Programming Language</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Platform">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">The operating system or hardware platform on which a software tool runs.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Platform</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>
